# Removed OpenClaw Skills

Generated from `https://github.com/openclaw/skills` git history.

This file lists root skill directories that have a `delete: skills/<owner>/<skill>` commit in history and whose root `SKILL.md` is not present in `HEAD`. It is sorted by removed date, newest first.

Total removed root skills found: 2074.

## Recovery

For any row below, recover the last version before deletion with:

```bash
git -C skills checkout <delete-commit>^ -- <skill-path>
```

For example, the zvec skill can be recovered with:

```bash
git -C skills checkout f36973c80e^ -- skills/emre-koc/zvec-local-rag-service
```
